\\t\\tdefault:\\n81: \\t\\t\\treturn nil, fmt.Errorf(\\\"unknown matcher type %q\\\", m.Type)\\n82: \\t\\t}\\n83: \\t\\tmatcher, err := labels.NewMatcher(mt, m.Name, m.Pattern)\\n84: \\t\\tif err != *slog.Logger\\n101: }\\n102: \\n103: // NewSilencer returns a new Silencer.\\n104: func NewSilencer(s *Silences, m types.AlertMarker, l *slog.Logger) *Silencer {\\n105: \\treturn &Silencer{\\n106: \\t\\tsilences: s,\\n107: \\t\\tmarker:   m,\\n108: \\t\\tlogger:   l,\\n109: \\t}\\n110: }\\n111: \\n112: // Mutes implements the Muter interface.\\n113: func (s *Silencer) Mutes(lset model.LabelSet) bool {\\n114: \\tfp := lset.Fingerprint()\\n115: \\tactiveIDs, pendingIDs, markerVersion, _ := s.marker.Silenced(fp)\\n116: \\n117: \\tvar (\\n118: \\t\\terr        error\\n119: \\t\\tallSils    []*pb.Silence\\n120: \\t\\tnewVersion = markerVersion\\n121: \\t)\\n122: \\tif markerVersion == s.silences.Version() {\\n123: \\t\\ttotalSilences := len(activeIDs) + len(pendingIDs)\\n124: \\t\\t// No new silences added, just need to check which of the old\\n125: \\t\\t// silences are still relevant and which of the pending ones\\n126: \\t\\t// have become active.\\n127: \\t\\tif totalSilences == 0 {\\n128: \\t\\t\\t// Super fast path: No silences ever applied to this\\n129: \\t\\t\\t// alert, none have been added. We are done.\\n130: \\t\\t\\treturn false\\n131: \\t\\t}\\n132: \\t\\t// This is still a quite fast path: No silences have been added,\\n133: \\t\\t// we only need to check which of the applicable silences are\\n134: \\t\\t// currently active. Note that newVersion is left at\\n135: \\t\\t// markerVersion because the Query call might already return a\\n136: \\t\\t// newer version, which is not the version our old list of\\n137: \\t\\t// applicable silences is based on.\\n138: \\t\\tallIDs := append(append(make([]string, 0, totalSilences), activeIDs...), pendingIDs...)\\n139: \\t\\tallSils, _, err = s.silences.Query(\\n140: \\t\\t\\tQIDs(allIDs...),\\n141: \\t\\t\\tQState(types.SilenceStateActive, types.SilenceStatePending),\\n142: \\t\\t)\\n143: \\t} else {\\n144: \\t\\t// New silences have been added, do a full query.\\n145: \\t\\tallSils, newVersion, err = s.silences.Query(\\n146: \\t\\t\\tQState(types.SilenceStateActive, types.SilenceStatePending),\\n147: \\t\\t\\tQMatches(lset),\\n148: \\t\\t)\\n149: \\t}\\n150: \\tif err != nil {\\n151: \\t\\ts.logger.Error(\\\"Querying silences failed, alerts might not get silenced correctly\\\", \\\"err\\\", err)\\n152: \\t}\\n153: \\tif len(allSils) == 0 {\\n154: \\t\\t// Easy case, neither active nor pending silences anymore.\\n155: \\t\\ts.marker.SetActiveOrSilenced(fp, newVersion, nil, nil)\\n156: \\t\\treturn false\\n157: \\t}\\n158: \\t// It is still possible that nothing has changed, but finding out is not\\n159: \\t// much less effort than just recreating the IDs from the query\\n160: \\t// result. Note that we cannot reuse the\\n161: \\t// current ID slices for concurrency reasons.\\n162: \\tactiveIDs, pendingIDs = nil, nil\\n163: \\tnow := s.silences.nowUTC()\\n164: \\tfor _, sil := range \\t}\\n174: \\ts.logger.Debug(\\n175: \\t\\t\\\"determined current silences state\\\",\\n176: \\t\\t\\\"now\\\", now,\\n177: \\t\\t\\\"total\\\", len(allSils),\\n178: \\t\\t\\\"active\\\", newVersion, activeIDs, pendingIDs)\\n185: \\n186: \\treturn len(activeIDs) > 0\\n187: }\\n188: \\n189: // Silences holds a silence state that can be modified, queried, and snapshot.\\n190: type {\\n596: \\ts.mtx.Lock()\\n597: \\tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\\n598: \\n599: \\tnow := s.nowUTC()\\n600: \\tif sil.StartsAt.IsZero() {\\n601: \\t\\tsil.StartsAt = now\\n602: \\t}\\n603: \\n604: \\tif err := {\\n128: \\t\\t\\t// Super fast path: No silences ever applied to this\\n129: \\t\\t\\t// alert, none have been added. We are done.\\n130: \\t\\t\\treturn false\\n131: \\t\\t}\\n132: \\t\\t// This is still a quite fast path: No silences have been added,\\n133: \\t\\t// we only need to check which of the applicable silences are\\n134: \\t\\t// currently active. Note that newVersion is left at\\n135: \\t\\t// markerVersion because the Query call might already return a\\n136: \\t\\t// newer version, which is not the version our old list of\\n137: \\t\\t// applicable silences is based on.\\n138: \\t\\tallIDs := append(append(make([]string, 0, totalSilences), activeIDs...), pendingIDs...)\\n139: \\t\\tallSils, _, err = s.silences.Query(\\n140: \\t\\t\\tQIDs(allIDs...),\\n141: \\t\\t\\tQState(types.SilenceStateActive, types.SilenceStatePending),\\n142: \\t\\t)\\n143: \\t} else {\\n144: \\t\\t// New silences have been added, do a full query.\\n145: \\t\\tallSils, newVersion, err = s.silences.Query(\\n146: \\t\\t\\tQState(types.SilenceStateActive, types.SilenceStatePending),\\n147: \\t\\t\\tQMatches(lset),\\n148: \\t\\t)\\n149: \\t}\\n150: \\tif err != nil {\\n151: \\t\\ts.logger.Error(\\\"Querying silences failed, alerts might not get silenced correctly\\\", \\\"err\\\", err)\\n152: \\t}\\n153: \\tif len(allSils) == 0 {\\n154: \\t\\t// Easy case, neither active nor pending silences anymore.\\n155: \\t\\ts.marker.SetActiveOrSilenced(fp, newVersion, nil, nil)\\n156: \\t\\treturn false\\n157: \\t}\\n158: \\t// It is still possible that nothing has changed, but finding out is not\\n159: \\t// much less effort than just recreating the IDs from the query\\n160: \\t// result. So let's do it in any case. Note that we cannot reuse the\\n161: \\t// current ID slices for concurrency reasons.\\n162: \\tactiveIDs, pendingIDs = nil, nil\\n163: \\tnow := s.silences.nowUTC()\\n164: \\tfor _, sil := range allSils {\\n165: \\t\\tswitch getState(sil, now) {\\n166: \\t\\tcase types.SilenceStatePending:\\n167: \\t\\t\\tpendingIDs = append(pendingIDs, sil.Id)\\n168: \\t\\tcase types.SilenceStateActive:\\n169: \\t\\t\\tactiveIDs = append(activeIDs, sil.Id)\\n170: \\t\\tdefault:\\n171: \\t\\t\\t// Do nothing, silence has expired in the meantime.\\n172: \\t\\t}\\n173: \\t}\\n174: \\ts.logger.Debug(\\n175: \\t\\t\\\"determined current silences state\\\",\\n176: \\t\\t\\\"now\\\", now,\\n177: \\t\\t\\\"total\\\", len(allSils),\\n178: \\t\\t\\\"active\\\", len(activeIDs),\\n179: \\t\\t\\\"pending\\\", len(pendingIDs),\\n180: \\t)\\n181: \\tsort.Strings(activeIDs)\\n182: \\tsort.Strings(pendingIDs)\\n183: \\n184: \\ts.marker.SetActiveOrSilenced(fp, newVersion, activeIDs, pendingIDs)\\n185: \\n186: \\treturn len(activeIDs) > 0\\n187: }\\n188: \\n189: // Silences holds a silence state that can be modified, queried, and snapshot.\\n190: type Silences struct {\\n191: \\tclock quartz.Clock\\n192: \\n193: \\tlogger    *slog.Logger\\n194: \\tmetrics   *metrics\\n195: \\tretention time.Duration\\n196: \\tlimits    Limits\\n197: \\n198: \\tmtx       sync.RWMutex\\n199: \\tst        state\\n200: \\tversion   int // Increments whenever silences are added.\\n201: \\tbroadcast func([]byte)\\n202: \\tmc        matcherCache\\n203: }\\n204: \\n205: // Limits contains the limits for silences.\\n206: type Limits struct {\\n207: \\t// MaxSilences limits the maximum number of silences, including expired\\n208: \\t// silences.\\n209: \\tMaxSilences func() int\\n210: \\t// MaxSilenceSizeBytes is the maximum size of an individual silence as\\n211: \\t// stored on disk.\\n212: \\tMaxSilenceSizeBytes func() int\\n213: }\\n214: \\n215: // MaintenanceFunc func() (int64, error)\\n218: \\n219: type metrics struct {\\n220: \\tgcDuration              prometheus.Summary\\n221: \\tsnapshotDuration        prometheus.Summary\\n222: If the snapshot\\n392: // file is set, a snapshot is written to it afterwards.\\n393: // Terminates on receiving from stopc.\\n394: // If not nil, the last argument is an override for what to do as part of the maintenance - for advanced usage.\\n395: func (s *Silences) Maintenance(interval time.Duration, snapf string, stopc <-chan struct{}, override MaintenanceFunc) {\\n396: \\tif interval == 0 || stopc == nil {\\n397: \\t\\ts.logger.Error(\\\"interval or stop signal are missing - not running maintenance\\\")\\n398: \\t\\treturn\\n399: \\t}\\n400: \\tt := s.clock.NewTicker(interval)\\n401: \\tdefer t.Stop()\\n402: \\n403: \\tvar doMaintenance MaintenanceFunc\\n404: \\tdoMaintenance = func() (int64, error) {\\n405: \\t\\tvar size int64\\n406: \\n407: \\t\\tif _, err := s.GC(); {\\n596: \\ts.mtx.Lock()\\n597: \\tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\\n598: \\n599: \\tnow := s.nowUTC()\\n600: \\tif sil.StartsAt.IsZero() {\\n601: \\t\\tsil.StartsAt = now\\n602: \\t}\\n603: \\n604: \\tif err := \\ts.mtx.Lock()\\n688: \\tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\\n689: \\treturn s.expire(id)\\n690: }\\n691: \\n692: // Expire the silence with the given ID immediately.\\n693: // It is idempotent, nil is returned if \tsilences *Silences\n99: \tmarker   types.AlertMarker\n100: \tlogger   *slog.Logger\n101: }\n102: \n103: // NewSilencer returns a new Silencer.\n104: func NewSilencer(s *Silences, m Muter interface.\n113: func (s *Silencer) Mutes(lset model.LabelSet) bool {\n114: \tfp := lset.Fingerprint()\n115: \tactiveIDs, pendingIDs, markerVersion, _ := s.marker.Silenced(fp)\n116: \n117: \tvar (\n118: \t\terr        error\n119: \t\tallSils    []*pb.Silence\n120: \t\tnewVersion = markerVersion\n121: \t)\n122: \tif markerVersion == s.silences.Version() {\n123: \t\ttotalSilences := len(activeIDs) + len(pendingIDs)\n124: \t\t// No new silences added, just need to check which of the old\n125: \t\t// silences are still relevant and which of the pending ones\n126: \t\t// have become active.\n127: \t\tif totalSilences == 0 {\n128: \t\t\t// Super fast path: No silences ever applied to this\n129: \t\t\t// alert, none have been added. We are done.\n130: \t\t\treturn false\n131: \t\t}\n132: \t\t// This is still a quite fast path: No silences have been added,\n133: \t\t// we only need to check which of the applicable silences are\n134: \t\t// currently active. Note that newVersion is left at\n135: \t\t// markerVersion because the Query call might already return a\n136: \t\t// newer version, which is not the version our old list of\n137: \t\t// applicable silences is based on.\n138: \t\tallIDs := append(append(make([]string, 0, totalSilences), activeIDs...), pendingIDs...)\n139: \t\tallSils, _, err = s.silences.Query(\n140: \t\t\tQIDs(allIDs...),\n141: \t\t\tQState(types.SilenceStateActive, types.SilenceStatePending),\n142: \t\t)\n143: \t} else {\n144: \t\t// New silences have been added, do a full query.\n145: \t\tallSils, newVersion, err = s.silences.Query(\n146: \t\t\tQState(types.SilenceStateActive, types.SilenceStatePending),\n147: \t\t\tQMatches(lset),\n148: \t\t)\n149: \t}\n150: \tif err != nil {\n151: \t\ts.logger.Error(\"Querying silences failed, alerts might not get silenced correctly\", \"err\", err)\n152: \t}\n153: \tif len(allSils) == 0 {\n154: \t\t// Easy case, neither active nor pending silences anymore.\n155: \t\ts.marker.SetActiveOrSilenced(fp, newVersion, nil, nil)\n156: \t\treturn false\n157: \t}\n158: \t// It is still possible that nothing has changed, but finding out is not\n159: \t// much less effort than just recreating the IDs from the query\n160: \t// result. So let's do it in any case. Note that we cannot reuse the\n161: \t// current ID slices for concurrency reasons.\n162: \tactiveIDs, pendingIDs = nil, nil\n163: \tnow := s.silences.nowUTC()\n164: \tfor _, sil := range allSils {\n165: \t\tswitch getState(sil, now) {\n166: \t\tcase types.SilenceStatePending:\n167: \t\t\tpendingIDs = append(pendingIDs, sil.Id)\n168: \t\tcase types.SilenceStateActive:\n169: \t\t\tactiveIDs = append(activeIDs, sil.Id)\n170: \t\tdefault:\n171: \t\t\t// Do nothing, silence has expired in the meantime.\n172: \t\t}\n173: \t}\n174: \ts.logger.Debug(\n175: \t\t\"determined current silences state\",\n176: \t\t\"now\", now,\n177: \t\t\"total\", len(allSils),\n178: \t\t\"active\", len(activeIDs),\n179: \t\t\"pending\", len(pendingIDs),\n180: \t)\n181: \tsort.Strings(activeIDs)\n182: \tsort.Strings(pendingIDs)\n183: \n184: \ts.marker.SetActiveOrSilenced(fp, newVersion, activeIDs, pendingIDs)\n185: \n186: \treturn len(activeIDs) > 0\n187: }\n188: \n189: // Silences holds a silence state that can be modified, queried, and snapshot.\n190: type Silences struct {\n191: \tclock quartz.Clock\n192: \n193: \tlogger    *slog.Logger\n194: \tmetrics   *metrics\n195: \tretention func([]byte)\n202: \tmc        matcherCache\n203: }\n204: \n205: // Limits contains the limits for silences.\n206: type Limits struct {\n207: \t// MaxSilences limits the maximum number of silences, taken or an error if it failed.\n217: type MaintenanceFunc func() (int64, error)\n218: \n219: type metrics struct {\n220: \tgcDuration              prometheus.Summary\n221: \tsnapshotDuration        prometheus.Summary\n222: \tsnapshotSize            prometheus.Gauge\n223: \tqueriesTotal            prometheus.Counter\n224: \tqueryErrorsTotal        prometheus.Counter\n225: \tqueryDuration {\n324: \t// A snapshot file or reader from which the initial state is loaded.\n325: \t// None or only one of them must be set.\n326: \tSnapshotFile   string\n327: \tSnapshotReader io.Reader\n328: \n329: \t// Retention time for newly created Silences. Silences may be\n330: \t// garbage collected after the given duration after they ended.\n331: \tRetention time.Duration\n332: \tLimits    Limits\n333: \n334: \t// A logger used by background processing.\n335: \tLogger  *slog.Logger\n336: \tMetrics prometheus.Registerer\n337: }\n338: \n339: func (o *Options) validate() error {\n340: \tif o.SnapshotFile != \"\" && o.SnapshotReader != nil {\n341: \t\treturn errors.New(\"only one of SnapshotFile and SnapshotReader must be set\")\n342: \t}\n343: \treturn nil\n344: }\n345: \n346: // New returns a new Silences object with the given configuration.\n347: func New(o Options) (*Silences, error) {\n348: \tif err := o.validate(); err != nil {\n349: \t\treturn nil, err\n350: \t}\n351: \n352: \ts := &Silences{\n353: \t\tclock:     quartz.NewReal(),\n354: \t\tmc:        matcherCache{},\n355: \t\tlogger:    promslog.NewNopLogger(),\n356: \t\tretention: o.Retention,\n357: \t\tlimits:    o.Limits,\n358: \t\tbroadcast: func([]byte) {},\n359: \t\tst:        state{},\n360: \t}\n361: \ts.metrics = newMetrics(o.Metrics, s)\n362: \n363: \tif o.Logger != nil {\n364: \t\ts.logger = o.Logger\n365: \t}\n366: \n367: \tif o.SnapshotFile != \"\" {\n368: \t\tif r, err := os.Open(o.SnapshotFile); err != nil {\n369: \t\t\tif !os.IsNotExist(err) {\n370: \t\t\t\treturn nil, err\n371: \t\t\t}\n372: \t\t\ts.logger.Debug(\"silences snapshot file doesn't exist\", \"err\", err)\n373: \t\t} else {\n374: \t\t\to.SnapshotReader = r\n375: \t\t\tdefer r.Close()\n376: \t\t}\n377: \t}\n378: \n379: \tif o.SnapshotReader != nil {\n380: \t\tif err := s.loadSnapshot(o.SnapshotReader); err != nil {\n381: \t\t\treturn s, err\n382: \t\t}\n383: \t}\n384: \treturn s, nil\n385: }\n386: \n387: func (s *Silences) nowUTC() time.Time {\n388: \treturn s.clock.Now().UTC()\n389: }\n390: \n391: // Maintenance garbage collects the silence state at the given interval. If the snapshot\n392: // file is set, a snapshot is written to it afterwards.\n393: // Terminates on receiving from stopc.\n394: // If not nil, the last argument is an override for what to do as part of the maintenance - for advanced usage.\n395: func (s *Silences) Maintenance(interval time.Duration, snapf string, stopc <-chan struct{}, override MaintenanceFunc) {\n396: \tif interval == 0 || stopc == nil {\n397: \t\ts.logger.Error(\"interval or stop signal are missing - not running maintenance\")\n398: \t\treturn\n399: \t}\n400: \tt := s.clock.NewTicker(interval)\n401: \tdefer t.Stop()\n402: \n403: \tvar doMaintenance MaintenanceFunc\n404: \tdoMaintenance = func() (int64, error) {\n405: \t\tvar size int64\n406: \n407: \t\tif _, err := s.GC(); err != nil {\n408: \t\t\treturn size, err\n409: \t\t}\n410: \t\tif snapf == \"\" {\n411: \t\t\treturn size, nil\n412: \t\t}\n413: \t\tf, err := openReplace(snapf)\n414: \t\tif err != nil {\n415: \t\t\treturn size, err\n416: \t\t}\n417: \t\tif size, err = s.Snapshot(f); err != nil {\n418: \t\t\tf.Close()\n419: \t\t\treturn size, err\n420: \t\t}\n421: \t\treturn size, f.Close()\n422: \t}\n423: \n424: \tif override != nil {\n425: \t\tdoMaintenance = override\n426: \t}\n427: \n428: \trunMaintenance := func(do MaintenanceFunc) error {\n429: \t\ts.metrics.maintenanceTotal.Inc()\n430: \t\ts.logger.Debug(\"Running maintenance\")\n431: \t\tstart := s.nowUTC()\n432: \t\tsize, err := do()\n433: \t\ts.metrics.snapshotSize.Set(float64(size))\n434: \t\tif err != nil {\n435: \t\t\ts.metrics.maintenanceErrorsTotal.Inc()\n436: \t\t\treturn err\n437: \t\t}\n438: \t\ts.logger.Debug(\"Maintenance done\", \"duration\", s.clock.Since(start), \"size\", size)\n439: \t\treturn nil\n440: \t}\n441: \n442: Loop:\n443: \tfor {\n444: \t\tselect {\n445: \t\tcase <-stopc:\n446: \t\t\tbreak Loop\n447: \t\tcase <-t.C:\n448: \t\t\tif err := runMaintenance(doMaintenance); err != nil {\n449: \t\t\t\t// @tjhop: this should probably log at error level\n450: \t\t\t\ts.logger.Info(\"Running maintenance failed\", \"err\", err)\n451: \t\t\t}\n452: \t\t}\n453: \t}\n454: \n455: \t// No need for final maintenance if we don't want to snapshot.\n456: \tif snapf == \"\" {\n457: \t\treturn\n458: \t}\n459: \tif err := runMaintenance(doMaintenance); err != nil {\n460: \t\t// @tjhop: this should probably log at error level\n461: \t\ts.logger.Info(\"Creating shutdown snapshot failed\", \"err\", err)\n462: \t}\n463: }\n464: \n465: // GC runs a garbage collection that removes silences that have ended longer\n466: // than the configured retention time ago.\n467: func (s *Silences) GC() (int, error) {\n468: \tstart := time.Now()\n469: \tdefer func() { s.metrics.gcDuration.Observe(time.Since(start).Seconds()) }()\n470: \n471: \tnow := s.nowUTC()\n472: \tvar n int\n473: \n474: \ts.mtx.Lock()\n475: \tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\n476: \n477: \tfor id, sil := range s.st {\n478: \t\tif sil.ExpiresAt.IsZero() {\n479: \t\t\treturn n, errors.New(\"unexpected zero expiration timestamp\")\n480: \t\t}\n481: \t\tif !sil.ExpiresAt.After(now) {\n482: \t\t\tdelete(s.st, id)\n483: \t\t\tdelete(s.mc, sil.Silence.Id)\n484: \t\t\tn++\n485: \t\t}\n486: \t}\n487: \n488: \treturn n, nil\n489: }\n490: \n491: func validateMatcher(m *pb.Matcher) error {\n492: \tif !compat.IsValidLabelName(model.LabelName(m.Name)) {\n493: \t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid label name %q\", m.Name)\n494: \t}\n495: \tswitch m.Type {\n496: \tcase pb.Matcher_EQUAL, pb.Matcher_NOT_EQUAL:\n497: \t\tif !model.LabelValue(m.Pattern).IsValid() {\n498: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid label value %q\", m.Pattern)\n499: \t\t}\n500: \tcase pb.Matcher_REGEXP, pb.Matcher_NOT_REGEXP:\n501: \t\tif _, err := regexp.Compile(m.Pattern); err != nil {\n502: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid regular expression %q: %w\", m.Pattern, err)\n503: \t\t}\n504: \tdefault:\n505: \t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"unknown matcher type %q\", m.Type)\n506: \t}\n507: \treturn nil\n508: }\n509: \n510: func matchesEmpty(m *pb.Matcher) bool {\n511: \tswitch m.Type {\n512: \tcase pb.Matcher_EQUAL:\n513: \t\treturn m.Pattern == \"\"\n514: \tcase pb.Matcher_REGEXP:\n515: \t\tmatched, _ := regexp.MatchString(m.Pattern, \"\")\n516: \t\treturn matched\n517: \tdefault:\n518: \t\treturn false\n519: \t}\n520: }\n521: \n522: func validateSilence(s *pb.Silence) error {\n523: \tif len(s.Matchers) == 0 {\n524: \t\treturn errors.New(\"at least one matcher required\")\n525: \t}\n526: \tallMatchEmpty := true\n527: \n528: \tfor i, m := range s.Matchers {\n529: \t\tif err := validateMatcher(m); err != nil {\n530: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid label matcher %d: %w\", i, err)\n531: \t\t}\n532: \t\tallMatchEmpty = allMatchEmpty && matchesEmpty(m)\n533: \t}\n534: \tif allMatchEmpty {\n535: \t\treturn errors.New(\"at least one matcher must not match the empty string\")\n536: \t}\n537: \tif s.StartsAt.IsZero() {\n538: \t\treturn errors.New(\"invalid zero start timestamp\")\n539: \t}\n540: \tif s.EndsAt.IsZero() {\n541: \t\treturn errors.New(\"invalid zero end timestamp\")\n542: \t}\n543: \tif s.EndsAt.Before(s.StartsAt) {\n544: \t\treturn errors.New(\"end time must not be before start time\")\n545: \t}\n546: \treturn nil\n547: }\n548: \n549: // cloneSilence returns a shallow copy of a silence.\n550: func cloneSilence(sil *pb.Silence) *pb.Silence {\n551: \ts := *sil\n552: \treturn &s\n553: }\n554: \n555: func (s *Silences) checkSizeLimits(msil *pb.MeshSilence) error {\n556: \tif s.limits.MaxSilenceSizeBytes != nil {\n557: \t\tn := msil.Size()\n558: \t\tif m := s.limits.MaxSilenceSizeBytes(); If a silence with the ID already exists and the modification\n594: // modifies history, the old silence gets expired and a new one is created.\n595: func (s *Silences) Set(sil *pb.Silence) error {\n596: \ts.mtx.Lock()\n597: \tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\n598: \n599: \tnow := s.nowUTC()\n600: \tif sil.StartsAt.IsZero() {\n601: \t\tsil.StartsAt = now\n602: \t}\n603: \n604: \tif err := validateSilence(sil); err != nil {\n605: \t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"invalid silence: %w\", err)\n606: \t}\n607: \n608: \tprev, ok := s.getSilence(sil.Id)\n609: \tif sil.Id != \"\" && !ok {\n610: \t\treturn ErrNotFound\n611: \t}\n612: \n613: \tif ok && canUpdate(prev, sil, now) {\n614: \t\tsil.UpdatedAt = now\n615: \t\tmsil := s.toMeshSilence(sil)\n616: \t\tif err := s.checkSizeLimits(msil); err != nil {\n617: \t\t\treturn err\n618: \t\t}\n619: \t\treturn s.setSilence(msil, now)\n620: \t}\n621: \n622: \t// If we got here it's either a new silence or a replacing one (which would\n623: \t// also create a new silence) so we need to make sure we have capacity for\n624: \t// the new silence.\n625: \tif s.limits.MaxSilences != nil {\n626: \t\tif m := s.limits.MaxSilences(); m > 0 && len(s.st)+1 > m {\n627: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"exceeded maximum number of silences: %d (limit: %d)\", len(s.st), m)\n628: \t\t}\n629: \t}\n630: \n631: \tuid, err := uuid.NewV4()\n632: \tif err != nil {\n633: \t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"generate uuid: %w\", err)\n634: \t}\n635: \tsil.Id = uid.String()\n636: \n637: \tif sil.StartsAt.Before(now) {\n638: \t\tsil.StartsAt = now\n639: \t}\n640: \tsil.UpdatedAt = now\n641: \n642: \tmsil := s.toMeshSilence(sil)\n643: \tif err := s.checkSizeLimits(msil); err != nil {\n644: \t\treturn err\n645: \t}\n646: \n647: \tif ok && getState(prev, s.nowUTC()) != types.SilenceStateExpired {\n648: \t\t// We cannot update the silence, expire the old one to leave a history of\n649: \t\t// the silence before modification.\n650: \t\tif err := s.expire(prev.Id); err != nil {\n651: \t\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"expire previous silence: %w\", err)\n652: \t\t}\n653: \t}\n654: \n655: \treturn s.setSilence(msil, now)\n656: }\n657: \n658: // canUpdate returns true if silence a can be updated to b without\n659: // affecting the historic view of silencing.\n660: func canUpdate(a, b *pb.Silence, now time.Time) bool {\n661: \tif !reflect.DeepEqual(a.Matchers, b.Matchers) {\n662: \t\treturn false\n663: \t}\n664: \t// Allowed timestamp modifications depend on the current time.\n665: \tswitch st := getState(a, now); st {\n666: \tcase types.SilenceStateActive:\n667: \t\tif b.StartsAt.Unix() != a.StartsAt.Unix() {\n668: \t\t\treturn false\n669: \t\t}\n670: \t\tif b.EndsAt.Before(now) {\n671: \t\t\treturn false\n672: \t\t}\n673: \tcase types.SilenceStatePending:\n674: \t\tif b.StartsAt.Before(now) {\n675: \t\t\treturn false\n676: \t\t}\n677: \tcase types.SilenceStateExpired:\n678: \t\treturn false\n679: \tdefault:\n680: \t\tpanic(\"unknown silence state\")\n681: \t}\n682: \treturn true\n683: }\n684: \n685: // Expire the silence with the given ID immediately.\n686: func (s *Silences) Expire(id string) error {\n687: \ts.mtx.Lock()\n688: \tdefer s.mtx.Unlock()\n689: \treturn s.expire(id)\n690: }\n691: \n692: // Expire the silence with the given ID immediately.\n693: // It is idempotent, nil is returned if the silence already expired before it is GC'd.\n694: // If the silence is not found an error is returned.\n695: func (s *Silences) expire(id string) error {\n696: \tsil, ok := s.getSilence(id)\n697: \tif !ok {\n698: \t\treturn ErrNotFound\n699: \t}\n700: \tsil = cloneSilence(sil)\n701: \tnow := s.nowUTC()\n702: \n703: \tswitch getState(sil, now) {\n704: \tcase types.SilenceStateExpired:\n705: \t\treturn nil\n706: \tcase types.SilenceStateActive:\n707: \t\tsil.EndsAt = now\n708: \tcase types.SilenceStatePending:\n709: \t\t// Set both to now to make Silence move to \"expired\" state\n710: \t\tsil.StartsAt = now\n711: \t\tsil.EndsAt = now\n712: \t}\n713: \tsil.UpdatedAt = now\n714: \treturn s.setSilence(s.toMeshSilence(sil), now)\n715: }\n716: \n717: // Final Notifier Dispatch (notify/notify.go:FanoutStage, line 488)**\\nThe FanoutStage executes all configured integrations for a receiver concurrently. Each integration's Notify() method is called to send the alert through the integration's notification channel (email, Slack, PagerDuty, etc.). The RetryStage handles exponential backoff and retry logic, with latency metrics recorded for each notification attempt.\\n\\nThe entire pipeline is orchestrated through the Stage interface and executed via MultiStage for sequential stages and FanoutStage for parallel execution.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":4,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3509,"cache_read_input_tokens":91574,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3509},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"927d4675-ac48-464a-a343-b8c7291a7f78","uuid":"ccd859f6-27b1-47ae-b5b5-e2dd5e80774c"}
